              <h2>
               Can You Guess The Harry Potter Movie From The Screenshot?
              </h2>
              <div class="headline-1 quiz_tally">
              </div>
              <ol>
               <li class="quiz_result has_result_image" data-id="3538840" rel:description='You must have been hit with the Obliviate charm because your "HP" movie knowledge is siriusly lacking.                  You must have been hit with the Obliviate charm because your HP movie knowledge is siriusly lacking. Why dont you treat yourself to a movie marathon  itll only take about 20 hours.

				}

					if (!('wid=13;page=1;sz=300x250;pos=bigstorybpage;tile=13;flex_medium=bigstory').match(/pos=300x250/) &amp;&amp; null !== window.location.search.match("skipdfp")) {

                          // this checks for lowes=calendar_sp (or anything matching the regex below)
                          // appends an extra tag
                          // to deliver a specific kind of ad for the lowes summer calendar program - see Jira card BF-17357
                          if(window.location.search.match('lowes') &amp;&amp; BF_STATIC.tt_page === "Buzz"){
                            if(window.location.search.match('lowes=calendar_sp')) ad_tag += 'lowes=calendar_sp;'
                            else if (window.location.search.match('lowes=carousel_edit')) ad_tag += 'lowes=carousel_edit;'
                          }

                          if(typeof GWI_AB_VARIATION !== "undefined" &amp;&amp; GWI_AB_VARIATION.length){
                                ad_tag += 'abtest=' + GWI_AB_VARIATION + ';';
                          }

				ad_tag += 'poe=' + BF_REFERER + ';';
				ad_tag += 'ord=' + BF_DFP_ORD + '?';
			
			ad_tag += ';large_images=1?';
			
				if (ad_tag) {
					if (!('wid=6;posnum=2;sz=3x3;pos=sidebar;tile=6').match(/pos=300x250/) &amp;&amp; null !== window.location.search.match("skipdfp")) {
						window.addEventListener('load', function(){
							var query = (typeof String.prototype.toQueryParams != 'undefined') ? window.location.search.toQueryParams() : $.deparam.querystring();
							var ad_user = (query['skipdfp']) ? query['skipdfp'] : 'boost';
							var extra_params = (/bigstory/.test('wid=6;posnum=2;sz=3x3;pos=sidebar;tile=6')) ? '&amp;flex_medium=bigstory' : '';
							local_ad_call( 6, ad_user, extra_params );
						})
					} else {
						if(!BF_STATIC.bf_test_mode || document.cookie.match('sel2_ad') !== null ) {
							document.write('&lt;'+'scr'+'ipt type="text/javascr'+'ipt" src="'+ad_tag+'"&gt;&lt;\/scr'+'ipt'+'&gt;');
						} else {
							console.info('disable DFP (dfp_tags.tt)');
						}
					}
				}
			
		    if (null !== window.location.search.match("adtest") &amp;&amp; console !== undefined &amp;&amp; typeof ad_tag != "undefined") console.log(ad_tag);
		}
